<h2 class='date-header'>
<span>
Monday, September 29, 2014
</span>
</h2>

                                        <div class="date-posts">
                                      
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iDkb49vxmW4/VCmt5gyLRTI/AAAAAAAAxRU/oo1_btlfqK0/s1600/images%2B(1).jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>

<a name='5759199288516958238'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/jonathan-places-pa-akinwunmi-on.html'>
Jonathan Places Pa Akinwunmi On Lifetime Salary And Gives Houses To Others (PHOTO)
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5759199288516958238' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iDkb49vxmW4/VCmt5gyLRTI/AAAAAAAAxRU/oo1_btlfqK0/s1600/images%2B(1).jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iDkb49vxmW4/VCmt5gyLRTI/AAAAAAAAxRU/oo1_btlfqK0/s1600/images%2B(1).jpg" height="400" width="318"></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">As a mark of appreciation to their dedication to service as well as to the nation, President Goodluck Jonathan has directed the Minister of FCT Senator Bala Mohammed to give out flats in Abuja to Traffic Warden Solomon Dauda, Taxi driver Imeh Usuah, as well as head of the Presidential stewards Onuh Isaac Micheal.</span><br>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"></span><br>
</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='jump-link'>

</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8505707372454611976' itemprop='articleBody'>

<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&#160;Less than two week after a church building collapsed in Benin, capital oof Edo State, another church building collapsed in the ancient city.</span><br>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/lagos-state-employs-80-female-lagbus.html'>
Lagos State Employs 80 Female LAGBUS Drivers
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5659138977395817313' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mGceoZ-jmD8/VCkfnwcE-WI/AAAAAAAAxO4/kMV5_8mQOvY/s1600/lagbus-600x320.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mGceoZ-jmD8/VCkfnwcE-WI/AAAAAAAAxO4/kMV5_8mQOvY/s1600/lagbus-600x320.jpg" height="212" width="400"></a></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Lagos State Government yesterday said it had employed additional 80 women as mass transit drivers, with Lagos Bus Asset Management Company, LAGBUS, as part of its effort to empower women in the state.</span></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/justin-bieber-shares-adorable-childhood.html'>
Justin Bieber Shares Adorable Childhood Photo Of Himself
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3912966835274765725' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-tTryyTzfJdw/VCa7L9XwFwI/AAAAAAAAxJ0/ZhypL6Fx-RI/s1600/1411792640321_wps_12_Justin_Bieber_Instagram_T.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-tTryyTzfJdw/VCa7L9XwFwI/AAAAAAAAxJ0/ZhypL6Fx-RI/s1600/1411792640321_wps_12_Justin_Bieber_Instagram_T.jpg" height="397" width="400"></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&#160;On Friday the 20-year-old posted a throwback snap of himself to Instagram showing him at a more innocent phase of his life, which quickly threw his fans into a giddy craze of adulation for the undeniably adorable portrait.</span><br>

Pregnant Alicia Keys Displays Baby Bump In New Photos
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7772119918895346542' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QLmnQgwo89M/VCa26nH8GSI/AAAAAAAAxJc/dMyTVYGEKxI/s1600/1411779940515_wps_40_Celebrities_rehearse_for_.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-QLmnQgwo89M/VCa26nH8GSI/AAAAAAAAxJc/dMyTVYGEKxI/s1600/1411779940515_wps_40_Celebrities_rehearse_for_.jpg" height="400" width="265"></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&#160;But not even pregnancy can stop Alicia Keys from lending her voice to a charitable cause.</span><br>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">On Friday, the 33-year-old looked blissful in a comfortable white top that hugged her growing belly as she rehearsed for Saturday&#39;s Global Citizen Festival in New York City.</span><br>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/projecting-feminine-essence-miss.html'>
Projecting The Feminine Essence - Miss Fotogenix Nigeria 2014 Calls For Entries!!!
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2677338920662379241' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QeohV7lAboM/VCZTerK2TsI/AAAAAAAAxI4/MkiV2sRiBZM/s1600/Miss%2BFotogenix%2BBanner.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QeohV7lAboM/VCZTerK2TsI/AAAAAAAAxI4/MkiV2sRiBZM/s1600/Miss%2BFotogenix%2BBanner.jpg" height="400" width="397"></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br></span>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">There is hardly any brand globally that has not in one way or the other, utilized the features exclusive to the female gender in a bid to try connect with its target audience or pass its brand message.</span><br>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br></span>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Hence, using photography as a vehicle, the Miss Fotogenix Nigeria Pageant is poised to empower a new crop of young, intelligent and beautiful ladies in view of harnessing their capacity through the grooming and projection of their innate and physical features as potential brand ambassadors.</span><br>
</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/id-el-kabir-fg-declares-october-6th-7th.html'>
Id-El-Kabir - FG Declares October 6th & 7th Public Holidays
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3494198423256610871' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Celp79lvm2I/VCZQT8xeM8I/AAAAAAAAxIc/8srmDuvknDA/s1600/goodluck_1636002c.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Celp79lvm2I/VCZQT8xeM8I/AAAAAAAAxIc/8srmDuvknDA/s1600/goodluck_1636002c.jpg" height="200" width="320" /></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">The Federal government of Nigeria has declared Monday October 6th and Tuesday October 7th as public holidays to mark the Islamic celebration, Id-El-Kabir&nbsp;</span><br />
<div>
<br /></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/has-god-cursed-nigeria-etcetera-writes.html'>
Has God Cursed Nigeria? - Etcetera Writes
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8737288114430515369' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0RfFbyzvsw4/VCZPt3gqYVI/AAAAAAAAxIU/9a5ESMWBmlI/s1600/Etcetera.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0RfFbyzvsw4/VCZPt3gqYVI/AAAAAAAAxIU/9a5ESMWBmlI/s1600/Etcetera.jpg" height="320" width="240"></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<br></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">I&#8217;ll like to state that I am writing as a Christian, and one who is tolerant of other beliefs. And I do not want this to be seen as a debate whether or not God exists. So, you religious hammer throwers should hold on. But feel free to read if you can shed your holier-than-thou skin momentarily, and see the premise of this write-up.</span><br>
</div>

</div>

<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IFxxceP1mVE/VCWCd2mlbjI/AAAAAAAAxHw/z7y_NaaLjL8/s1600/Abducted-Chibok-school-grils-360x225.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IFxxceP1mVE/VCWCd2mlbjI/AAAAAAAAxHw/z7y_NaaLjL8/s1600/Abducted-Chibok-school-grils-360x225.jpg" height="250" width="400"></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">The abducted &#8220;Chibok girl&#8221; released on Wednesday is &#8220;pregnant and mentally ill,&#8221; the National Chairman of Chibok Community Development Association, Dr. Pogu Bitrus, has told TheCable.</span><br>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/jason-durelo-confirms-split-from-jordin.html'>
Jason Durelo Confirms Split From Jordin Sparks After 3 Years 
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4886734858408361107' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--BHcSaGmV3g/VCWAdQjt9aI/AAAAAAAAxHg/XA03oIb_cSM/s1600/1411703638074_wps_36_Mandatory_Credit_Photo_by.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--BHcSaGmV3g/VCWAdQjt9aI/AAAAAAAAxHg/XA03oIb_cSM/s1600/1411703638074_wps_36_Mandatory_Credit_Photo_by.jpg" height="400" width="243" /></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;Singers Jordin Sparks and Jason Derulo have broken up.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">After reports initially started doing the rounds on Thursday morning, the 25-year-old singer confirmed the news during a radio interview with KDWB in Minneapolis that afternoon.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">And while he admitted that the long-time couple have indeed parted ways, he insisted there is no bad blood between them.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">'Everything is cool man. It's not a bad situation, it's not one of those kinds of things,' he said.</span><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<br /></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.lazywrita.com/2014/09/mayhem-in-ekiti-over-murder-of-nurtw.html'>
Mayhem In Ekiti Over Murder Of NURTW chairman (PHOTOS)
</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4998630674331442236' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hcKjKMqf078/VCV-c2TuzCI/AAAAAAAAxHI/gMb4-9eE5OY/s1600/Untitled.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hcKjKMqf078/VCV-c2TuzCI/AAAAAAAAxHI/gMb4-9eE5OY/s1600/Untitled.png" height="236" width="400"></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&#160;Thugs are said to be causing rampage in Ekiti after the assassination of &#160;former chairman of the National Union of Road Transport Workers (NURTW) in Ekiti State, Mr. Omolafe Aderiye .</span><br>
<span style="font-family: Helvetica Neue, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Another photo after the cut</span><br>
</div>
